style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The Canary Wharf Group (comprising Canary Wharf Group plc and its\nsubsidiaries) manages its<a></a> operations on a unified basis.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>For this reason, the company's directors\nbelieve that key<a></a> performance indicators specific to the\ncompany are not necessary or appropriate for an<a></a> understanding\nof the development, performance or position of its business.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The performance<a></a> of the Canary\nWharf Group, which includes the company, is discussed in the Annual Report of<a></a> Canary Wharf Group plc, which does not form part of this\nreport.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">DIVIDENDS AND RESERVES</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The profit and loss account for the year ended\n31 December 2012 is set out on page </span><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-no-proof:yes\">8</span></span><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><a></a>. No<a></a> dividends have been paid or proposed (2011: Nil) and the\nretained loss of 9,027,022 (2011: profit of 2,144,706) has been transferred\nto reserves.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">GOING CONCERN</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">As a result of a reduction in the value of its property interests,\nthe company is in a net<a></a> liability position at the year end.\nHowever, the company has the benefit of leases which<a></a> provide\nan income stream which the directors forecast will enable it to meet its<a></a> obligations as they fall due for a period of not less than 12\nmonths from the signing date<a></a> of the financial statements. In\naddition, as a member of the Canary Wharf Group, the company has access to\nconsiderable resources.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quotquot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Having made the requisite enquiries, the directors have a\nreasonable expectation that the<a></a> company will have adequate\nresources to continue its operations for the foreseeable future.<a></a>\nAccordingly they continue to adopt the going concern basis in preparing the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection4\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The company provides an indemnity to all directors (to the extent\npermitted by law) in<a></a> respect of liabilities incurred as a\nresult of their office.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The company also\nhas in place<a></a> liability insurance covering the directors and\nofficers of the company.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Both the\nindemnity<a></a> and insurance were in force during the year ended\n31 December 2012 and at the time of the<a></a> approval of\nthis Directors' Report.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Neither the\nindemnity nor the insurance provide cover<a></a> in the event that\nthe director is proven to have acted dishonestly or fraudulently.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">PRINCIPAL RISKS AND UNCERTAINTIES</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">As a member of the Canary Wharf Group the key risks facing the\ncompany include<a></a> the cyclical nature of the property market,\nfinancing risk and concentration risk.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Cyclical Nature of the Property Market</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The valuation of the Canary Wharf Group's assets is subject to\nmany external economic and<a></a> market factors. The turmoil in the\nfinancial markets and uncertainty in the Eurozone in recent years has been\nreflected in the property market by such factors as a significant decline in\ntenant demand for space in London, the oversupply of available space in the\noffice market and changing market perceptions of property as an investment\nresulting in variations in property valuations in general. Fears of an\noversupply of available space in the market have however been mitigated by the\ndifficulty in securing finance for speculative development and reduced supply.\nThe market has also been assisted by the continuing presence of overseas\ninvestors attracted by the relative transparency of the real estate market in\nLondon which is still viewed as both stable and secure. Changes in financial\nand property markets are kept under constant review so that the company can\nreact appropriately and tailor its business accordingly.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>While the company has no direct exposure to the\nEuro, the ongoing uncertainty reflecting issues in the macroeconomy,\nparticularly relating to the Eurozone, continues to impact the real estate\nmarket.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The impact of these\nuncertainties is closely monitored.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Financing Risk</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The broader economic cycle inevitably leads to movements in inflation,\ninterest rates and<a></a> bond yields. The company finances its\noperations largely through surplus cash and<a></a> intercompany\nfinance.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The terms of the company's\nborrowings are summarised in Note 9.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The ongoing uncertainty in financial markets continues to\nsignificantly limit the<a></a> availability of funding. In common\nwith other UK property companies, lack of financing<a></a>\nfacilities may have an impact on the business of Canary Wharf Group if the\nlending markets<a></a> remain limited for the foreseeable future.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></b><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></b></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Concentration Risk</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The majority of Canary Wharf Group's real estate assets, including\nthe assets of the<a></a> company, are currently located on or\nadjacent to the Canary Wharf Estate with a majority of<a></a>\ntenants linked to the financial services industry.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Wherever possible steps are taken to<a></a> mitigate or avoid material consequences arising from this\nconcentration and to diversify<a></a> the tenant base.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The principal risks facing the Canary Wharf Group are discussed in\nthe Annual Report of<a></a> Canary Wharf Group plc, which does not\nform part of this report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Company law requires the\n directors to prepare financial statements for each financial year.<a></a> Under that law the directors have elected to prepare the\n financial statements in accordance<a></a> with United Kingdom\n Generally Accepted Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a></a> Standards and applicable law). Under company law the\n directors must not approve the financial statements unless they are satisfied\n that they give a true and fair view of the state of affairs of the company and\n of the profit or loss of the company for that period.<a></a> In\n preparing these financial statements, the directors are required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; and</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">The directors are\n responsible for keeping proper accounting records that disclose with<a></a> reasonable accuracy at any time the financial position of the\n company and enable them to ensure that the financial statements comply with\n the Companies Act 2006. They are also responsible for safeguarding the assets\n of the company and hence for taking reasonable steps for the prevention and\n detection of fraud and other irregularities.</span><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and\ndisclosures in the financial<a></a> statements sufficient to give\nreasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a>\nfrom material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a>\nof: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's\ncircumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> annual report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we consider<a></a> the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>PRINCIPAL\nACCOUNTING POLICIES</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>A\nsummary of the principal accounting policies of the company, all of which have\nbeen<a></a> applied consistently throughout the year and the\npreceding year, is set out below.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Accounting\nconvention</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:StatementOnBasisMeasurementPreparationAccounts\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>The financial statements have been\n prepared under the historical cost convention, modified to include the\n revaluation of properties and in accordance with applicable United Kingdom\n accounting standards. The financial statements have been prepared on the going\n concern basis</span></ix:nonNumeric></span> as described in the Directors' Report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>In\naccordance with the provisions of FRS 1 (Revised) the company is exempt from<a></a> the requirements to prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a\nwholly-owned<a></a> subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has\nprepared a consolidated cash flow<a></a> statement.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Turnover</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Turnover represents rents\n receivable net of VAT and is recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\n which the rents become due.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Interest\nreceivable and interest payable</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest\nreceivable and payable are recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\nwhich they fall due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investment\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment\nproperties are revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for\nInvestment Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure\nfrom the requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all\nproperties to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for\nthe accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the\nfactors reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this\nfactor is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses\nor deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit exceeds\nprevious surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the excess is\ncharged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective\nevidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according\nto the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other creditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade\nand other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Debt</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt\ninstruments are stated initially at the amount of the net proceeds. The finance\ncosts of such debt instruments are allocated to periods over the term of the\ndebt at a constant rate on the carrying amount. The carrying amount is\nincreased by the finance cost in respect of the reporting period and reduced by\npayments made in respect of the debt of that period. Finance costs are charged\nto the profit and loss account.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection12\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the recognition\nof gains and losses in the financial statements and their recognition in the\ncorporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is\nestimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing\ndifferences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years. <span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on\ngovernment bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the\ndeferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>OPERATING PROFIT</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Operating\nprofit is stated after charging:</span></p><table
